This page lists the IAM roles and permissions for Gemini Enterprise for Customer Experience. To search through all roles and permissions, see the [role and permission index](https://docs.cloud.google.com/iam/docs/roles-permissions) .

### Service agent roles

Service agent roles should only be granted to [service agents](https://docs.cloud.google.com/iam/docs/service-agents) .

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="header">
<th>Role</th>
<th>Permissions</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="odd">
<td><h4 id="ces.serviceAgent" class="role-title add-link" data-text="Customer Engagement Suite Service Agent" tabindex="-1">Customer Engagement Suite Service Agent</h4>
<p>( <code dir="ltr" translate="no">roles/  ces.serviceAgent</code> )</p>
<p>Allows Customer Engagement Suite Service Account to access to dependent resources.</p>
<blockquote>
<strong>Warning:</strong> Do not grant service agent roles to any principals except <a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/iam/docs/service-agents">service agents</a> .
</blockquote></td>
<td><p><code dir="ltr" translate="no">aiplatform.endpoints.get</code></p>
<p><code dir="ltr" translate="no">aiplatform.endpoints.predict</code></p>
<p><code dir="ltr" translate="no">aiplatform.extensions.execute</code></p>
<p><code dir="ltr" translate="no">aiplatform.extensions.get</code></p>
